doth ech parte devyde subtill fro groce fro thyck thyn separacyon manuall look thou put asyde pertaynyth folys whych lyttyll good wyn separacyon nature doth blyn makyng dyvysyon qualytes elementall fyfth degree tyll turned erth y turnyd water black bloe water ayre whyte ayre y turned fyre element mo thys y made crafte stone grete delyte thys separacyon much must wryte separacyon y callyd phylosophers dyffynycyon sayd element tetraptatyve dyspersyon thys separacyon fynde lyke fygure thus spoken prophet yn psalmody god brought stone flud water pure hardyst stone oyle abundantly ryght precyose stone yf thou wytty oyle incombusteble water thou shalt draw thereabout thou nedyst cole blow thys wyth hete esy mesuryng fyrst wyth moyst fyre wyth dry flewme pacyence owt drawyng thy nature wyttyly dry thyne erth tyll hyt thrysty calcenyng el thou laboryst vayne make hyt drynke moysture agayne separacyon thus must thou ofte tymes make thy matter dyvydyng part two symple fro groce thou take tyll erth remayne benethe color bloe erth y fyx abyde wo parte y spyrytuall fleyng thou must turne hem one thyng oyle water wyth water shall dystyll thorow help receve menyng kepe well thys two thou spyll thy wark lack dew closyng make thy stopell glas meltyng top thy vessle together wyth yt phylosopherlyke usyd y hyt water wherwyth thou must renew thy stone looke thou dystyll afore thou warke wyth hyt oftentymes selfe alone thy syght thou shalt well wyt fro feculent feces hyt y quytt sum men wyth saturne multeply substance defye dystyll hyt therfore tyll hyt clene thyn lyke water hyt shold hevyn color bryght shyne kepyng fygure ponderosyte therwith dyd hermes moysture hys tre wythyn hys glas made grow upryght wyth flower dyscoloryd bewtyosely syght thys water y lyke venemous tyre wherewyth myghty tryacle y wrought yt y poyson stronge yre stronger poyson none thought att potecarys therfore oftyn yt y bought man shall hyt intoxycate tyme yt y medycyne elevate y tryacall trew hyt y poysons expulsyfe hys working doth mervells shewe preservyng many deth lyfe loke thou meng yt wyth corrosyve chese hyt pure quick rennyng yf thou thereby wylt wynnyng y mervelose thyng kynde wythout hyt may nought done therefore hermes calleth hyt hys wynde y flying fro sonn mone makyth stone flye wyth hyt sone revyvyng ded gevyng lyfe son mone husband wyfe whych yf craft made quick ther fatnes wyth water drawn thyn dyssevered thyke thou never bryng thys worke yf thou wylt speed therefore wythout doubt reyse thy byrd theyre nest agayne bryng downe rest water wyth water accord wyll assend spryt wyth spryt kynde whych exalted make dyssend soe thou shalt devyde nature dyd bynde mercury essencyall turnyng wynde wythout whych naturall subtyll seperacyon may never compleat profytable generacyon help thee thys gate last secret wyll tell thee thy water must seven tymes sublymate ell shall kyndly dyssolucyon putryfyyng shall thou none see like lyquyd pytch colour apperyng lack fyre temperance never may among repugnance thus causyth separacion trew conjunccion water ayre earth fyre every element may lad abyde ever thy desyre done laborous clay myer temper thyke make thyn drying rejoysyth wyth refrygeracion tell kepe hyt therfore wyth temperat hete adowne full forty dayes tyll hyt wex black abowen sowle begynnyth com owte fro hys owne vaynys subtyll y wyll wyth spryts assend dowte sublymyng esyly manner water doth hym bere ayre one chyld thus must bore water ageyne seyd sublymacyon continuall laboryd wyth hete moyst temperate y whyte purely made spirituall hevyn uppon fermentyng dyvers maners y whych medcyns must perpetuate clere water som lesyth son mone wyth ther medcyns makyth congelate whych fyer tyme examynate may abyde alter wyth complement ferment y intent yet kyndly som men fermentyng theyer medcynes thys wyse mercury dyssolvyng son mone wyth spryts tyll tyme wyll aryse sublymyng together twyse thryse fermentacyon therof make y way yet hyt forsake som
